                                                                                                var previousSearchKeyword = '';
                                                                                                predictionRequest = function(isOnPageLoad) {
                                                                                                    let keyword = A.one('input.search-bar-keywords-input').val();
                                                                                                    if (keyword.length >= 3 && previousSearchKeyword !== keyword) {
                                                                                                        previousSearchKeyword = keyword;
                                                                                                        A.io.request('https://irdai.gov.in/rules?p_p_id=com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch&p_p_lifecycle=2&p_p_state=normal&p_p_mode=view&p_p_resource_id=%2Fsearch%2Fpredictions&p_p_cacheability=cacheLevelPage', {
                                                                                                            method: 'post',
                                                                                                            dataType: 'json',
                                                                                                            data: {
                                                                                                                _com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch_searchKeyword: keyword
                                                                                                            },
                                                                                                            on: {
                                                                                                                success: function() {
                                                                                                                    let responseData = this.get('responseData');
                                                                                                                    let predictionHtml = '';
                                                                                                                    if (!isOnPageLoad && responseData.length > 0) {
                                                                                                                        A.one('#_com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch_searchTopics').show();
                                                                                                                    } else {
                                                                                                                        A.one('#_com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch_searchTopics').hide();
                                                                                                                    }
                                                                                                                    responseData.forEach(function(item) {
                                                                                                                        let optText = '<div class="border-bottom text-sm" onclick="searchByPrediction(\`' + item.title + '\`)"><small><b>' + item.title + '</b></small></div>';
                                                                                                                        predictionHtml += optText;
                                                                                                                    });
                                                                                                                    A.one('#searchPredictions').setHTML(predictionHtml);
                                                                                                                },
                                                                                                                failure: function() {
                                                                                                                    console.log('request Failed');
                                                                                                                }
                                                                                                            }
                                                                                                        });
                                                                                                    } else if (keyword.length < 3) {
                                                                                                        previousSearchKeyword = keyword;
                                                                                                        A.one('#searchPredictions').setHTML('<span class="bg-muted test-muted"></span>');
                                                                                                        2
                                                                                                        A.one('#_com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch_searchTopics').hide();
                                                                                                    }
                                                                                                }
                                                                                                searchByPrediction = function(predictionKeyword) {
                                                                                                    A.one('input.search-bar-keywords-input').val(predictionKeyword);
                                                                                                    A.one('form#_com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch_fm').simulate('submit');
                                                                                                    A.one('#_com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch_searchTopics').hide(true);
                                                                                                }
                                                                                                Liferay.on('allPortletsReady', function() {
                                                                                                    var searchInputNode = A.one('input.search-bar-keywords-input');
                                                                                                    var searchFormNode = A.one('form');
                                                                                                    var searchTopicsNode = A.one('#_com_liferay_portal_search_web_search_bar_portlet_SearchBarPortlet_INSTANCE_templateSearch_searchTopics');
                                                                                                    searchTopicsNode.setXY([searchInputNode.getX(), (searchInputNode.getY() + searchInputNode.height() + 17)]);
                                                                                                    searchTopicsNode.hide();
                                                                                                    searchTopicsNode.removeClass('invisible');
                                                                                                    /*searchFormNode.on('focus', function(event){						
                                                                                                    	searchTopicsNode.show(true);
                                                                                                    });*/
                                                                                                    if (searchInputNode.val() && searchInputNode.val() != '') {
                                                                                                        predictionRequest(true);
                                                                                                    }
                                                                                                    A.one('body').on('click', function(event) {
                                                                                                        let searchAreaXStart = searchInputNode.getX();
                                                                                                        let searchAreaXEnd = searchAreaXStart + searchTopicsNode.width();
                                                                                                        let searchAreaYStart = searchInputNode.getY();
                                                                                                        let searchAreaYEnd = searchAreaYStart + searchInputNode.height() + searchTopicsNode.height() + 10;
                                                                                                        if (event.clientX < searchAreaXStart || event.clientX > searchAreaXEnd || event.clientY < searchAreaYStart || event.clientY > searchAreaYEnd) {
                                                                                                            searchTopicsNode.hide(true);
                                                                                                        }
                                                                                                    });
                                                                                                    var searchKeyTimeOut;
                                                                                                    searchInputNode.on('keyup', function(event) {
                                                                                                        if (searchKeyTimeOut) clearTimeout(searchKeyTimeOut);
                                                                                                        searchKeyTimeOut = setTimeout(predictionRequest, 500);
                                                                                                    });
                                                                                                });
                                                                                            }
                                                                                            let searchTopicCount = 0;
                                                                                            A.all('.search-topics').each(function() {
                                                                                                if (searchTopicCount > 0) {
                                                                                                    this.remove();
                                                                                                }
                                                                                                searchTopicCount++;
                                                                                            });
                                                                                        })();
                                                                                    });
                                                                                    // ]]>
                                                                        </script>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                </div>
                                                            </div>
                                                        </section>
                                                    </div>
                                                </div>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                                                                            <script>
                                                                                var pageLink = "https://irdai.gov.in/rules"
                                                                                var pageTitle = String(document.title).replace(/\&/g, '%26');

                                                                                function fbk_click() {
                                                                                    window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=' + pageLink + '&quote=' + pageTitle, 'sharer', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=626,height=436');
                                                                                    return false;
                                                                                }

                                                                                function twt_click() {
                                                                                    window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=' + pageTitle + '&url=' + pageLink, 'sharer', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=626,height=436');
                                                                                    return false;
                                                                                }

                                                                                function lnk_click() {
                                                                                    window.open('https://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle/?url=' + pageLink, 'sharer', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=626,height=436');
                                                                                    return false;
                                                                                }

                                                                                function what_click() {
                                                                                    window.open('https://api.whatsapp.com/send?text=' + pageLink, 'sharer', 'toolbar=0,width=626,height=436');
                                                                                    return false;
                                                                                }

                                                                                function email_click() {
                                                                                    var pageLinkUrl = "https://irdai.gov.in/rules?p_p_id=com_irdai_share_IrdaiShareModulePortlet_INSTANCE_ZUiEj2DcOXSj&p_p_lifecycle=0&p_p_state=pop_up&p_p_mode=view&_com_irdai_share_IrdaiShareModulePortlet_INSTANCE_ZUiEj2DcOXSj_mvcPath=%2FsharePage.jsp&url=" + pageLink;
                                                                                    Liferay.Util.openWindow({
                                                                                        dialog: {
                                                                                            centered: true,
                                                                                            height: 960,
                                                                                            modal: true,
                                                                                            width: 500,
                                                                                            cssClass: "ui-model",
                                                                                            destroyOnHide: true,
                                                                                            resizable: false,
                                                                                        },
                                                                                        title: "EMAIL THIS PAGE",
                                                                                        centered: true,
                                                                                        id: '_com_irdai_share_IrdaiShareModulePortlet_INSTANCE_ZUiEj2DcOXSj_mailPopup',
                                                                                        uri: pageLinkUrl
                                                                                    });
                                                                                }
                                                                                $(".shareBlock a.share").click(function(e) {
                                                                                    $('.shareBlock').show();
                                                                                    $('.shareList').toggle();
                                                                                    e.preventDefault();
                                                                                });
                                                                                $(document).mouseup(function(e) {
                                                                                    var container = $(".shareBlock a.share");
                                                                                    // if the target of the click isn't the container nor a descendant of the container
                                                                                    if (!container.is(e.target) && container.has(e.target).length === 0) {
                                                                                        $(".shareList").hide();
                                                                                    }
                                                                                });
                                                                            </script>

                                                                    <script>
                                                                        function onlyOne(checkbox) {
                                                                            var checkboxes = document.getElementsByName('_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterArchive');
                                                                            checkboxes.forEach((item) => {
                                                                                if (item !== checkbox) item.checked = false
                                                                            })
                                                                        }

                                                                    $(document).ready(function() {
                                                                        $('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterClear, #_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterApply').removeClass('btn-secondary');
                                                                        setTimeout(500, function() {
                                                                            $("th.title-head").trigger('click');
                                                                        });
                                                                        $("#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_cbSelectAll").click(function(event) {
                                                                            if (this.checked) {
                                                                                $(".checkSingle").each(function() {
                                                                                    this.checked = true;
                                                                                })
                                                                            } else {
                                                                                $(".checkSingle").each(function() {
                                                                                    this.checked = false;
                                                                                })
                                                                            }
                                                                        });
                                                                        $(".checkSingle").click(function() {
                                                                            if ($(this).is(":checked")) {
                                                                                var isAllChecked = 0;
                                                                                $(".checkSingle").each(function() {
                                                                                    if (!this.checked) isAllChecked = 1;
                                                                                })
                                                                                if (isAllChecked == 0) {
                                                                                    $("#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_cbSelectAll").prop("checked", true);
                                                                                }
                                                                            } else {
                                                                                $("#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_cbSelectAll").prop("checked", false);
                                                                            }
                                                                        });
                                                                    });
                                                                </script>

            var pageLink = window.location.href;
            var pageTitle = String(document.title).replace(/\&/g, '%26');

            function fbs_click() {
                window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=' + pageLink + '&quote=' + pageTitle, 'sharer', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=626,height=436');
                return false;
            }

            function tbs_click() {
                window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?text=' + pageTitle + '&url=' + pageLink, 'sharer', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=626,height=436');
                return false;
            }

            function lbs_click() {
                window.open('https://www.linkedin.com/sharing/share-offsite/?url=' + pageLink, 'sharer', 'toolbar=0,status=0,width=626,height=436');
                return false;
            }

            function rbs_click() {

                return false;
            }

            function wha_click() {

                return false;
            }

                                            $(function() {
                                                $(document).ready(function() {
                                                    if (document.getElementById('Mumbai')) {
                                                        $('#Mumbai').show();
                                                    } else if (document.getElementById('मुंबई')) {
                                                        $('#मुंबई').show();
                                                    }
                                                });
                                                $('#location').change(function() {
                                                    if ($('#location').val() == 'Mumbai') {
                                                        $('#Mumbai').show();
                                                        $('#Delhi').hide();
                                                    } else if ($('#location').val() == 'Delhi') {
                                                        $('#Mumbai').hide();
                                                        $('#Delhi').show();
                                                    } else if ($('#location').val() == 'दिल्ली') {
                                                        $('#मुंबई').hide();
                                                        $('#दिल्ली').show();
                                                    } else if ($('#location').val() == 'मुंबई') {
                                                        $('#मुंबई').show();
                                                        $('#दिल्ली').hide();
                                                    }
                                                });
                                            });
                                        </script>

                        function handleDownloadClick(event) {
                            if (event.target.nodeName.toLowerCase() === 'a' && window.Analytics) {
                                var anchor = event.target;
                                var match = pathnameRegexp.exec(anchor.pathname);

                                        });
                                        return result;
                                    };

                        (function() {
                            var $ = AUI.$;
                            var _ = AUI._;
                            A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterApply').on('click', function(event) {
                                let departmentKeyword = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterDepartment').val();
                                let fromDateKeyword = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterFromDate').val();
                                let toDateKeyword = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterToDate').val();
                                let searchKeyword = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterSearchKeyword').val();
                                const today = new Date();
                                var initial = fromDateKeyword.split(/\//);
                                var initialFrom = [initial[1], initial[0], initial[2]].join('/');
                                var initial1 = toDateKeyword.split(/\//);
                                var initialTo = [initial1[1], initial1[0], initial1[2]].join('/');
                                if (fromDateKeyword != null || toDateKeyword != null) {
                                    if (new Date(initialFrom) > today || new Date(initialTo) > today) {
                                        document.getElementById('todateValidationMsg').innerHTML = "Please Select Correct Dates";
                                        return false;
                                    } else {
                                        document.getElementById('todateValidationMsg').innerHTML = "";
                                    }
                                    if (new Date(initialFrom) > new Date(initialTo)) {
                                        document.getElementById('todateValidationMsg').innerHTML = "To Date Should Less Than From Date";
                                        return false;
                                    } else {
                                        document.getElementById('todateValidationMsg').innerHTML = "";
                                    }
                                }
                                let entitiesKeyword = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterEntities').val();
                                let classificationKeyword = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterClassification').val();
                                let tagKeyword = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterTag').val();
                                let archiveOn = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterArchiveInclude').attr('checked');
                                let archiveOnly = A.one('#_com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet_filterArchiveOnly').attr('checked');
                                let filterUrl = Liferay.PortletURL.createRenderURL();
                                filterUrl.setPortletId('com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet');
                                filterUrl.setParameter('filterDepartment', departmentKeyword);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('filterFromDate', fromDateKeyword);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('filterToDate', toDateKeyword);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('filterSearchKeyword', searchKeyword);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('filterEntities', entitiesKeyword);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('filterClassification', classificationKeyword);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('filterTag', tagKeyword);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('archiveOn', archiveOn);
                                filterUrl.setParameter('archiveOnly', archiveOnly);
                                window.location.assign(filterUrl.toString());
                            });
                        })();

                                if (selectedBoxes.size() > 0) {
                                    let selectedFileEntries = [];

                                    let downloadAllUrl = Liferay.PortletURL.createResourceURL();
                                    downloadAllUrl.setPortletId('com_irdai_document_media_IRDAIDocumentMediaPortlet');
                                    downloadAllUrl.setResourceId("downloadAll");
                                    downloadAllUrl.setParameter("selectedEntries", selectedFileEntriesValue);
                                    downloadAllUrl.setParameter("zipFileName", document.title);

        <script>
            $(document).ready(function() {
                var resize = new Array('p', '.resizable', 'div', 'span', 'h4', 'h5', 'h6', 'button', 'img', 'li', 'td', 'th', 'a', 'marquee', 'small');
                resize = resize.join(',');
                //resets the font size when "reset" is clicked
                var resetFont = $(resize).css('font-size');
                $(".reset").click(function() {
                    // window.location.reload();
                    window.location.href = window.location.href;
                });
                //increases font size when "+" is clicked
                $(".increase").click(function() {
                    var originalFontSize = $(resize).css('font-size');
                    var originalFontNumber = parseFloat(originalFontSize, 10);
                    var newFontSize = originalFontNumber * 1.1;
                    $(resize).css('font-size', newFontSize);
                    var sizeh1 = $("h1").css("font-size");
                    var sizeh1 = parseInt(sizeh1, 10);
                    var newsizeh1 = sizeh1 * 1.1;
                    var sizeh2 = $("h2").css("font-size");
                    var sizeh2 = parseInt(sizeh2, 10);
                    var newsizeh2 = sizeh2 * 1.1;
                    var sizeh3 = $("h3").css("font-size");
                    var sizeh3 = parseInt(sizeh3, 10);
                    var newsizeh3 = sizeh3 * 1.1;
                    console.log(sizeh2);
                    $("h2").css("font-size", newsizeh2);
                    $("h3").css("font-size", newsizeh3);
                    $("h1").css("font-size", newsizeh1);
                    return false;
                });
                //decrease font size when "-" is clicked
                $(".decrease").click(function() {
                    var originalFontSize = $(resize).css('font-size');
                    var originalFontNumber = parseFloat(originalFontSize, 10);
                    var newFontSize = originalFontNumber * 0.9;
                    $(resize).css('font-size', newFontSize);
                    var sizeh1 = $("h2").css("font-size");
                    var sizeh1 = parseInt(sizeh1, 10);
                    var newsizeh1 = sizeh1 * 0.9;
                    var sizeh2 = $("h2").css("font-size");
                    var sizeh2 = parseInt(sizeh2, 10);
                    var newsizeh2 = sizeh2 * 0.9;
                    var sizeh3 = $("h3").css("font-size");
                    var sizeh3 = parseInt(sizeh3, 10);
                    var newsizeh3 = sizeh3 * 0.9;
                    console.log(newsizeh3);
                    $("h2").css("font-size", newsizeh2);
                    $("h3").css("font-size", newsizeh3);
                    $("h1").css("font-size", newsizeh1);
                    return false;
                });
            });
            $('#zoom-in').click(function() {
                updateZoom(0.1);
            });
            zoomLevel = 1;
            var updateZoom = function(zoom) {
                zoomLevel += zoom;
                $('body').css({
                    zoom: zoomLevel,
                    '-moz-transform': 'scale(' + zoomLevel + ')'
                });
            }
            $('#grey').click(function() {
                $("div").removeClass("lightTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("lightTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("light");
                $("span").removeClass("light");
                $("div").removeClass("negativeTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("negativeTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("negative");
                $("span").removeClass("negative");
                $("div").removeClass("highTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("highTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("high");
                $("span").removeClass("high");
                $("body").toggleClass("greyTheme");
                // document.getElementById("senna_surface1").style.filter = "grayscale(100%)";
            });
            $('#high').click(function() {
                $("div").removeClass("lightTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("lightTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("light");
                $("span").removeClass("light");
                $("div").removeClass("negativeTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("negativeTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("negative");
                $("span").removeClass("negative");
                $("div").toggleClass("highTheme");
                $("section").toggleClass("highTheme");
                $("a").toggleClass("high");
                $("span").toggleClass("high");
                $("body").removeClass("greyTheme");
            });
            $('#negative').click(function() {
                $("div").removeClass("highTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("highTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("high");
                $("span").removeClass("high");
                $("div").removeClass("lightTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("lightTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("light");
                $("span").removeClass("light");
                $("div").toggleClass("negativeTheme");
                $("section").toggleClass("negativeTheme");
                $("a").toggleClass("negative");
                $("span").toggleClass("negative");
                $("body").removeClass("greyTheme");
                //document.getElementById("senna_surface1").style.filter = "invert(100%)";
                //document.getElementByClassName("bg-green-light").style.background = "none";
                //document.getElementByClassName("bg-green-dark").style.background = "none";
            });
            $('#underline').click(function() {
                $('a').toggleClass("underlineThenme");
            });
            $('#readbleFont').click(function() {
                $("div").toggleClass("readbleFontTheme");
            });
            $('#light').click(function() {
                $("div").removeClass("highTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("highTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("high");
                $("span").removeClass("high");
                $("div").removeClass("negativeTheme");
                $("section").removeClass("negativeTheme");
                $("a").removeClass("negative");
                $("span").removeClass("negative");
                $("div").toggleClass("lightTheme");
                $("section").toggleClass("lightTheme");
                $("a").toggleClass("light");
                $("span").toggleClass("light");
                $("body").removeClass("greyTheme");
            });
            $('a[target="_external"]').click(function(event) {
                event.preventDefault();
                redirectExternal($(this).attr('href'));
            });
        </script>
        <script>
            function languageChangeAlertMsgHindi(url) {
                if (confirm('Are you sure you want to change the language to Hindi ?')) {
                    window.location.href = url;
                    //window.open(url, '_blank').focus();
                    // return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }

            function languageChangeAlertMsgEnglish(url) {
                if (confirm('क्या आप सुनिश्चित हैं कि आप भाषा को अंग्रेजी में बदलना चाहते हैं?')) {
                    window.location.href = url;
                    //window.open(url, '_blank').focus();
                    // return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }

            function redirectExternal(url) {
                if ((url.indexOf("https://agencyportal.irdai.gov.in/Index.htm") != -1)) {
                    window.open(url, '_blank').focus();
                } else {
                    if (confirm('You are now leaving the IRDAI Website ...The link you have selected is located on another server. Please click on OK to leave the IRDAI site and proceed to the selected site. IRDAI does not endorse this web site, its sponsor, or any of the policies, activities, products, or services offered on the site or by any advertiser on the site.')) {
                        window.open(url, '_blank').focus();
                        // return true;
                    } else {
                        return false;
                    }
                }
            }
        </script>
        <script>
            var language = "en_US";

            function languageChangeAlertMsg(url) {
                var message = "";
                console.log(language);
                if (language == "en_US") {
                    message = "Are you sure you want to change the language to Hindi ?";
                } else {
                    message = "Are you sure you want to change the language to English ?";
                }
                if (confirm(message)) {
                    window.location.href = url;
                    //window.open(url, '_blank').focus();
                    // return true;
                } else {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        </script>

        <script>
            var language = "en_US";
            var synthesizer = "";
            var speech = "";
            var stopClick = false;
            var speechSynthesisLanguage = "";
            var speechSynthesisVoiceName = "";
            var player = "";
            if (language == "en_US") {
                speechSynthesisLanguage = "en-IN";
                speechSynthesisVoiceName = "Microsoft Server Speech Text to Speech Voice (en-IN, NeerjaNeural)";
            } else if (language == "hi_IN") {
                speechSynthesisLanguage = "hi-IN";
                speechSynthesisVoiceName = "Microsoft Server Speech Text to Speech Voice (hi-IN, SwaraNeural)";
            }
            player = new SpeechSDK.SpeakerAudioDestination();
            var val = $("#audiocontent").val();
            if (val.includes("/home")) {
                var audioIdhome = document.getElementById("wrapper");
                if (audioIdhome) {
                    speech = document.getElementById("wrapper").innerText;
                    speech = speech.replace(/\n/g, " ");
                }
            } else {
                var audioinnerPage = document.getElementById("column-2");
                if (audioinnerPage) {
                    speech = document.getElementById("column-2").innerText;
                    speech = speech.replace(/\n/g, " ");
                }
            }
            $('#PauseBtn').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            $('#resumeButton').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            $('#stop').attr('disabled', 'disabled');

            function synthesizeSpeech() {
                $('#resumeButton').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                $('#PauseBtn').removeAttr('disabled');
                $('#stop').removeAttr('disabled');
                const speechConfig = SpeechSDK.SpeechConfig.fromSubscription("8d6cd31f5ceb435fafdb3be6ed608b51", "centralindia");
                // Note: if only language is set, the default voice of that language is chosen.
                speechConfig.speechSynthesisLanguage = speechSynthesisLanguage; // e.g. "de-DE"
                // The voice setting will overwrite language setting.
                // The voice setting will not overwrite the voice element in input SSML.
                speechConfig.speechSynthesisVoiceName = speechSynthesisVoiceName;
                speechConfig.setProperty("Transfer-Encoding", "chunked");
                speechConfig.speechSynthesisOutputFormat = "Webm24kzh16BitMomoOpus";
                var audioConfig = SpeechSDK.AudioConfig.fromSpeakerOutput(player);
                console.log("audioConfig", audioConfig);
                console.log("speechConfig", speechConfig);
                console.log("audioConfig", audioConfig);
                synthesizer = new SpeechSDK.SpeechSynthesizer(speechConfig, audioConfig);
                console.log("synthesizer", synthesizer);
                console.log("player", player);
                stopClick = false;
                const complete_cb = function(result) {
                    synthesizer.close();
                    synthesizer = undefined;
                };
                const err_cb = function(err) {
                    synthesizer.close();
                    synthesizer = undefined;
                };
                synthesizer.speakTextAsync(speech, complete_cb, err_cb);
                $('#start').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
            }
            $('#resumeButton').click(function() {
                $('#PauseBtn').removeAttr('disabled');
                $('#stop').removeAttr('disabled');
                $('#start').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                $('#resumeButton').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                if (stopClick == false) {
                    player.resume();
                }
            });
            $('#PauseBtn').click(function() {
                $('#resumeButton').removeAttr('disabled');
                $('#start').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                $('#PauseBtn').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                $('#stop').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                if (stopClick == false) {
                    player.pause();
                }
            });
            $('#stop').click(function() {
                stopAudio();
            });
            $('a').click(function(e) {
                if (e.currentTarget.href != "javascript:void(0)") {
                    stopAudio();
                }
            });

            function stopAudio() {
                $('#start').removeAttr('disabled');
                $('#PauseBtn').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                $('#resumeButton').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                $('#stop').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
                if (stopClick == false) {
                    stopClick = true
                    player.pause();
                    synthesizer = "";
                    player = new SpeechSDK.SpeakerAudioDestination();
                }
            }
        </script>
    </body>
</html>
